\DoxyCodeLine{3565 \textcolor{comment}{// Shaders management}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3566 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3567 \textcolor{comment}{// Load shader from code strings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3568 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: If shader string is NULL, using default vertex/fragment shaders}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3569 \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rlLoadShaderCode(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *vsCode, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *fsCode)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3570 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3571     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} \textcolor{keywordtype}{id} = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3572 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3573 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_33) || defined(GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_ES2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3574     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} vertexShaderId = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3575     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} fragmentShaderId = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3576 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3577     \textcolor{comment}{// Compile vertex shader (if provided)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3578     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (vsCode != NULL) vertexShaderId = rlCompileShader(vsCode, GL\_VERTEX\_SHADER);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3579     \textcolor{comment}{// In case no vertex shader was provided or compilation failed, we use default vertex shader}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3580     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (vertexShaderId == 0) vertexShaderId = RLGL.State.defaultVShaderId;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3581 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3582     \textcolor{comment}{// Compile fragment shader (if provided)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3583     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (fsCode != NULL) fragmentShaderId = rlCompileShader(fsCode, GL\_FRAGMENT\_SHADER);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3584     \textcolor{comment}{// In case no fragment shader was provided or compilation failed, we use default fragment shader}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3585     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (fragmentShaderId == 0) fragmentShaderId = RLGL.State.defaultFShaderId;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3586 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3587     \textcolor{comment}{// In case vertex and fragment shader are the default ones, no need to recompile, we can just assign the default shader program id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3588     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((vertexShaderId == RLGL.State.defaultVShaderId) \&\& (fragmentShaderId == RLGL.State.defaultFShaderId)) \textcolor{keywordtype}{id} = RLGL.State.defaultShaderId;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3589     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3590     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3591         \textcolor{comment}{// One of or both shader are new, we need to compile a new shader program}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3592         \textcolor{keywordtype}{id} = rlLoadShaderProgram(vertexShaderId, fragmentShaderId);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3593 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3594         \textcolor{comment}{// We can detach and delete vertex/fragment shaders (if not default ones)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3595         \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: We detach shader before deletion to make sure memory is freed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3596         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (vertexShaderId != RLGL.State.defaultVShaderId)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3597         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3598             glDetachShader(\textcolor{keywordtype}{id}, vertexShaderId);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3599             glDeleteShader(vertexShaderId);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3600         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3601         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (fragmentShaderId != RLGL.State.defaultFShaderId)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3602         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3603             glDetachShader(\textcolor{keywordtype}{id}, fragmentShaderId);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3604             glDeleteShader(fragmentShaderId);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3605         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3606 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3607         \textcolor{comment}{// In case shader program loading failed, we assign default shader}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3608         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{id} == 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3609         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3610             \textcolor{comment}{// In case shader loading fails, we return the default shader}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3611             TRACELOG(RL\_LOG\_WARNING, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}SHADER: Failed to load custom shader code, using default shader"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{3612             \textcolor{keywordtype}{id} = RLGL.State.defaultShaderId;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3613         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3614         \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3615 \textcolor{comment}{        else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3616 \textcolor{comment}{        \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3617 \textcolor{comment}{            // Get available shader uniforms}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3618 \textcolor{comment}{            // NOTE: This information is useful for debug...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3619 \textcolor{comment}{            int uniformCount = -\/1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3620 \textcolor{comment}{            glGetProgramiv(id, GL\_ACTIVE\_UNIFORMS, \&uniformCount);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3621 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3622 \textcolor{comment}{            for (int i = 0; i < uniformCount; i++)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3623 \textcolor{comment}{            \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3624 \textcolor{comment}{                int namelen = -\/1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3625 \textcolor{comment}{                int num = -\/1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3626 \textcolor{comment}{                char name[256] = \{ 0 \};     // Assume no variable names longer than 256}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3627 \textcolor{comment}{                GLenum type = GL\_ZERO;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3628 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3629 \textcolor{comment}{                // Get the name of the uniforms}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3630 \textcolor{comment}{                glGetActiveUniform(id, i, sizeof(name) -\/ 1, \&namelen, \&num, \&type, name);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3631 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3632 \textcolor{comment}{                name[namelen] = 0;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3633 \textcolor{comment}{                TRACELOGD("{}SHADER: [ID \%i] Active uniform (\%s) set at location: \%i"{}, id, name, glGetUniformLocation(id, name));}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3634 \textcolor{comment}{            \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3635 \textcolor{comment}{        \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3636 \textcolor{comment}{        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3637     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3638 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3639 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3640     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} id;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3641 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3642 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3643 \textcolor{comment}{// Compile custom shader and return shader id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3644 \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rlCompileShader(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *shaderCode, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} type)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3645 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3646     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} shader = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3647 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3648 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_33) || defined(GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_ES2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3649     shader = glCreateShader(type);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3650     glShaderSource(shader, 1, \&shaderCode, NULL);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3651 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3652     GLint success = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3653     glCompileShader(shader);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3654     glGetShaderiv(shader, GL\_COMPILE\_STATUS, \&success);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3655 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3656     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (success == GL\_FALSE)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3657     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3658         \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (type)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3659         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3660             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} GL\_VERTEX\_SHADER: TRACELOG(RL\_LOG\_WARNING, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}SHADER: [ID \%i] Failed to compile vertex shader code"{}}, shader); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3661             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} GL\_FRAGMENT\_SHADER: TRACELOG(RL\_LOG\_WARNING, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}SHADER: [ID \%i] Failed to compile fragment shader code"{}}, shader); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3662             \textcolor{comment}{//case GL\_GEOMETRY\_SHADER:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3663 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#if defined(GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_43)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3664             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} GL\_COMPUTE\_SHADER: TRACELOG(RL\_LOG\_WARNING, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}SHADER: [ID \%i] Failed to compile compute shader code"{}}, shader); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3665 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3666             \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3667         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3668 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3669         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} maxLength = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3670         glGetShaderiv(shader, GL\_INFO\_LOG\_LENGTH, \&maxLength);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3671 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3672         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (maxLength > 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3673         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3674             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} length = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3675             \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *log = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *)RL\_CALLOC(maxLength, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3676             glGetShaderInfoLog(shader, maxLength, \&length, log);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3677             TRACELOG(RL\_LOG\_WARNING, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}SHADER: [ID \%i] Compile error: \%s"{}}, shader, log);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3678             RL\_FREE(log);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3679         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3680     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3681     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3682     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3683         \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (type)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3684         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3685             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} GL\_VERTEX\_SHADER: TRACELOG(RL\_LOG\_INFO, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}SHADER: [ID \%i] Vertex shader compiled successfully"{}}, shader); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3686             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} GL\_FRAGMENT\_SHADER: TRACELOG(RL\_LOG\_INFO, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}SHADER: [ID \%i] Fragment shader compiled successfully"{}}, shader); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3687             \textcolor{comment}{//case GL\_GEOMETRY\_SHADER:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3688 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#if defined(GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_43)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3689             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} GL\_COMPUTE\_SHADER: TRACELOG(RL\_LOG\_INFO, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}SHADER: [ID \%i] Compute shader compiled successfully"{}}, shader); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3690 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3691             \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3692         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3693     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3694 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3695 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3696     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} shader;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3697 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3698 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3699 \textcolor{comment}{// Load custom shader strings and return program id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3700 \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rlLoadShaderProgram(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} vShaderId, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} fShaderId)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3701 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3702     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} program = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3703 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3704 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_33) || defined(GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_ES2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3705     GLint success = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3706     program = glCreateProgram();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3707 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3708     glAttachShader(program, vShaderId);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3709     glAttachShader(program, fShaderId);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3710 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3711     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Default attribute shader locations must be binded before linking}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3712     glBindAttribLocation(program, 0, RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_POSITION);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3713     glBindAttribLocation(program, 1, RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_TEXCOORD);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3714     glBindAttribLocation(program, 2, RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_NORMAL);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3715     glBindAttribLocation(program, 3, RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_COLOR);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3716     glBindAttribLocation(program, 4, RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_TANGENT);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3717     glBindAttribLocation(program, 5, RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_TEXCOORD2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3718 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3719     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: If some attrib name is no found on the shader, it locations becomes -\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3720 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3721     glLinkProgram(program);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3722 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4504 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_11)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4505 \textcolor{comment}{// Mipmaps data is generated after image data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4506 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Only works with RGBA (4 bytes) data!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4507 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rlGenTextureMipmapsData(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *data, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} baseWidth, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} baseHeight)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4508 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4509     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} mipmapCount = 1;                \textcolor{comment}{// Required mipmap levels count (including base level)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4510     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} width = baseWidth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4511     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} height = baseHeight;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4512     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} size = baseWidth*baseHeight*4;  \textcolor{comment}{// Size in bytes (will include mipmaps...), RGBA only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4513 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4514     \textcolor{comment}{// Count mipmap levels required}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4515     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} ((width != 1) \&\& (height != 1))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4516     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4517         width /= 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4518         height /= 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4519 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4520         TRACELOGD(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}TEXTURE: Next mipmap size: \%i x \%i"{}}, width, height);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4521 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4522         mipmapCount++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4523 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4524         size += (width*height*4);       \textcolor{comment}{// Add mipmap size (in bytes)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4525     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4526 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4527     TRACELOGD(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}TEXTURE: Total mipmaps required: \%i"{}}, mipmapCount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4528     TRACELOGD(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}TEXTURE: Total size of data required: \%i"{}}, size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4529 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4530     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *temp = RL\_REALLOC(data, size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4531 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4532     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (temp != NULL) data = temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4533     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} TRACELOG(RL\_LOG\_WARNING, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}TEXTURE: Failed to re-\/allocate required mipmaps memory"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4534 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4535     width = baseWidth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4536     height = baseHeight;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4537     size = (width*height*4);    \textcolor{comment}{// RGBA: 4 bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4538 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4539     \textcolor{comment}{// Generate mipmaps}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4540     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Every mipmap data is stored after data (RGBA -\/ 4 bytes)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4541     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *image = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *)RL\_MALLOC(width*height*4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4542     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *mipmap = NULL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4543     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} offset = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4544 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4545     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; i < size; i += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4546     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4547         image[i] = data[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4548         image[i + 1] = data[i + 1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4549         image[i + 2] = data[i + 2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4550         image[i + 3] = data[i + 3];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4551     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4552 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4553     TRACELOGD(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}TEXTURE: Mipmap base size (\%ix\%i)"{}}, width, height);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4554 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4555     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} mip = 1; mip < mipmapCount; mip++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4556     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4557         mipmap = rlGenNextMipmapData(image, width, height);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4558 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4559         offset += (width*height*4); \textcolor{comment}{// Size of last mipmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4560 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4561         width /= 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4562         height /= 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4563         size = (width*height*4);    \textcolor{comment}{// Mipmap size to store after offset}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4564 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4565         \textcolor{comment}{// Add mipmap to data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4566         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; i < size; i += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4567         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4568             data[offset + i] = mipmap[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4569             data[offset + i + 1] = mipmap[i + 1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4570             data[offset + i + 2] = mipmap[i + 2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4571             data[offset + i + 3] = mipmap[i + 3];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4572         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4573 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4574         RL\_FREE(image);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4575 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4576         image = mipmap;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4577         mipmap = NULL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4578     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4579 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4580     RL\_FREE(mipmap);       \textcolor{comment}{// free mipmap data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4581 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4582     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} mipmapCount;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4583 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4584 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4585 \textcolor{comment}{// Manual mipmap generation (basic scaling algorithm)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4586 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *rlGenNextMipmapData(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *srcData, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} srcWidth, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} srcHeight)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4587 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4588     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x2 = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4589     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y2 = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4590     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} prow[4] = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4591     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} pcol[4] = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4592 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4593     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} width = srcWidth/2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4594     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} height = srcHeight/2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4595 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4596     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *mipmap = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *)RL\_MALLOC(width*height*4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4597 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4598     \textcolor{comment}{// Scaling algorithm works perfectly (box-\/filter)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4599     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y = 0; y < height; y++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4600     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4601         y2 = 2*y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4602 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4603         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x = 0; x < width; x++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4604         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4605             x2 = 2*x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4606 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4607             prow[0] = (srcData[(y2*srcWidth + x2)*4 + 0] + srcData[(y2*srcWidth + x2 + 1)*4 + 0])/2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4608             prow[1] = (srcData[(y2*srcWidth + x2)*4 + 1] + srcData[(y2*srcWidth + x2 + 1)*4 + 1])/2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4609             prow[2] = (srcData[(y2*srcWidth + x2)*4 + 2] + srcData[(y2*srcWidth + x2 + 1)*4 + 2])/2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4610             prow[3] = (srcData[(y2*srcWidth + x2)*4 + 3] + srcData[(y2*srcWidth + x2 + 1)*4 + 3])/2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4611 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4612             pcol[0] = (srcData[((y2 + 1)*srcWidth + x2)*4 + 0] + srcData[((y2 + 1)*srcWidth + x2 + 1)*4 + 0])/2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4613             pcol[1] = (srcData[((y2 + 1)*srcWidth + x2)*4 + 1] + srcData[((y2 + 1)*srcWidth + x2 + 1)*4 + 1])/2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4614             pcol[2] = (srcData[((y2 + 1)*srcWidth + x2)*4 + 2] + srcData[((y2 + 1)*srcWidth + x2 + 1)*4 + 2])/2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4615             pcol[3] = (srcData[((y2 + 1)*srcWidth + x2)*4 + 3] + srcData[((y2 + 1)*srcWidth + x2 + 1)*4 + 3])/2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4616 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4617             mipmap[(y*width + x)*4 + 0] = (prow[0] + pcol[0])/2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4618             mipmap[(y*width + x)*4 + 1] = (prow[1] + pcol[1])/2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4619             mipmap[(y*width + x)*4 + 2] = (prow[2] + pcol[2])/2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4620             mipmap[(y*width + x)*4 + 3] = (prow[3] + pcol[3])/2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4621         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4622     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4623 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4624     TRACELOGD(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}TEXTURE: Mipmap generated successfully (\%ix\%i)"{}}, width, height);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4625 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4626     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} mipmap;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4627 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4628 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif  }\textcolor{comment}{// GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_11}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4629 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4630 \textcolor{comment}{// Get pixel data size in bytes (image or texture)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4631 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Size depends on pixel format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4632 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rlGetPixelDataSize(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} width, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} height, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} format)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4633 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4634     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} dataSize = 0;       \textcolor{comment}{// Size in bytes}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4652         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} RL\_PIXELFORMAT\_COMPRESSED\_ETC2\_RGB:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4653         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} RL\_PIXELFORMAT\_COMPRESSED\_PVRT\_RGB:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4654         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} RL\_PIXELFORMAT\_COMPRESSED\_PVRT\_RGBA: bpp = 4; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4655         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} RL\_PIXELFORMAT\_COMPRESSED\_DXT3\_RGBA:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4656         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} RL\_PIXELFORMAT\_COMPRESSED\_DXT5\_RGBA:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4657         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} RL\_PIXELFORMAT\_COMPRESSED\_ETC2\_EAC\_RGBA:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4658         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} RL\_PIXELFORMAT\_COMPRESSED\_ASTC\_4x4\_RGBA: bpp = 8; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4659         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} RL\_PIXELFORMAT\_COMPRESSED\_ASTC\_8x8\_RGBA: bpp = 2; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4660         \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4661     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4662 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4663     dataSize = width*height*bpp/8;  \textcolor{comment}{// Total data size in bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4664 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4665     \textcolor{comment}{// Most compressed formats works on 4x4 blocks,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4666     \textcolor{comment}{// if texture is smaller, minimum dataSize is 8 or 16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4667     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((width < 4) \&\& (height < 4))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4668     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4669         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((format >= RL\_PIXELFORMAT\_COMPRESSED\_DXT1\_RGB) \&\& (format < RL\_PIXELFORMAT\_COMPRESSED\_DXT3\_RGBA)) dataSize = 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4670         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((format >= RL\_PIXELFORMAT\_COMPRESSED\_DXT3\_RGBA) \&\& (format < RL\_PIXELFORMAT\_COMPRESSED\_ASTC\_8x8\_RGBA)) dataSize = 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4671     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4672 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4673     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} dataSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4674 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4675 }
